   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Daylight saving time by country</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r992277484">.mw-parser-output .stack-container{box-sizing:border-box}.mw-parser-output .stack-clear-left{float:left;clear:left}.mw-parser-output .stack-clear-right{float:right;clear:right}.mw-parser-output .stack-left{float:left}.mw-parser-output .stack-right{float:right}.mw-parser-output .stack-margin-clear-left{float:left;clear:left;margin-right:1em}.mw-parser-output .stack-margin-clear-right{float:right;clear:right;margin-left:1em}.mw-parser-output .stack-margin-left{float:left;margin-right:1em}.mw-parser-output .stack-margin-right{float:right;margin-left:1em}.mw-parser-output .stack-container>div{margin:1px;overflow:hidden}@media all and (max-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .stack-container{float:none;width:100%}}</style>
      <div class="mw-stack stack-container stack-right">
       <div> 
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;">
          <a href="/wiki/File:DST_Countries_Map.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/DST_Countries_Map.png/400px-DST_Countries_Map.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="200" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/DST_Countries_Map.png/600px-DST_Countries_Map.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/DST_Countries_Map.png/800px-DST_Countries_Map.png 2x" data-file-width="4972" data-file-height="2492"></a> 
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a href="/wiki/File:DST_Countries_Map.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
           </div>Daylight saving time by country as of March&nbsp;2020<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Daylight_saving_time_by_country&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup> 
           <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r981673959">.mw-parser-output .legend{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .legend-color{display:inline-block;min-width:1.25em;height:1.25em;line-height:1.25;margin:1px 0;text-align:center;border:1px solid black;background-color:transparent;color:black}.mw-parser-output .legend-text{}</style>
           <div class="legend">
            <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#1a80e6; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/Northern_Hemisphere" title="Northern Hemisphere">Northern Hemisphere</a> summer
           </div> 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
           <div class="legend">
            <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#ee690a; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/Southern_Hemisphere" title="Southern Hemisphere">Southern Hemisphere</a> summer
           </div> 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
           <div class="legend">
            <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#7f7f7f; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Never used daylight saving
           </div> 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
           <div class="legend">
            <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#c6c6c6; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Formerly used daylight saving
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div> 
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Most areas in <a href="/wiki/Summer_time_in_Europe" title="Summer time in Europe">Europe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_in_the_Americas#North_America" title="Daylight saving time in the Americas">North America</a> observe <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time" title="Daylight saving time">daylight saving time</a> (DST), whereas most areas of <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_in_Africa" title="Daylight saving time in Africa">Africa</a> and <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_in_Asia" title="Daylight saving time in Asia">Asia</a> do not. In <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_in_the_Americas#South_America" title="Daylight saving time in the Americas">South America</a>, most countries in the north of the continent near the <a href="/wiki/Equator" title="Equator">Equator</a> do not observe DST, whereas <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a> and most of <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> do. The practice of observing daylight saving time in <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_in_Oceania" title="Daylight saving time in Oceania">Oceania</a> is also mixed, with <a href="/wiki/Time_in_New_Zealand#Daylight_saving_time_(DST)" title="Time in New Zealand">New Zealand</a> and parts of southeastern <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_in_Australia" title="Daylight saving time in Australia">Australia</a> observing DST, while most other areas do not. </p> 
      <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r886050035">.mw-parser-output .tocleft{float:left;clear:left;width:auto;background:none;padding:.5em .8em 1.4em 0;margin-bottom:.5em}.mw-parser-output .tocleft-clear-left{clear:left}.mw-parser-output .tocleft-clear-both{clear:both}.mw-parser-output .tocleft-clear-none{clear:none}</style>

           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_in_Mexico" title="Daylight saving time in Mexico">Daylight saving time in Mexico</a>
          </div> <p>Has observed DST since 1996, but <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Flag_of_Baja_California.svg/23px-Flag_of_Baja_California.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Flag_of_Baja_California.svg/35px-Flag_of_Baja_California.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Flag_of_Baja_California.svg/46px-Flag_of_Baja_California.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="350" data-file-height="200">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Baja_California" title="Baja California">Baja California</a> has observed DST since 1976. <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Flag_of_Sonora.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sonora.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Flag_of_Sonora.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sonora.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Flag_of_Sonora.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sonora.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="350" data-file-height="200">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Sonora" title="Sonora">Sonora</a> discontinued the observance in 1997 and <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Flag_of_Quintana_Roo.svg/23px-Flag_of_Quintana_Roo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Flag_of_Quintana_Roo.svg/35px-Flag_of_Quintana_Roo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Flag_of_Quintana_Roo.svg/46px-Flag_of_Quintana_Roo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="350" data-file-height="200">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Quintana_Roo" title="Quintana Roo">Quintana Roo</a> in 2014. Durango, Coahuila, Nuevo León and Tamaulipas observed DST in 1988. Locations less than 20&nbsp;km from the US border use U.S. DST. <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Flag_of_Baja_California.svg/23px-Flag_of_Baja_California.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Flag_of_Baja_California.svg/35px-Flag_of_Baja_California.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Flag_of_Baja_California.svg/46px-Flag_of_Baja_California.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="350" data-file-height="200">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Baja_California" title="Baja California">Baja California</a> also uses the U.S. DST.<sup id="cite_ref-Cetram_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cetram-6">[6]</a></sup> </p> </td>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Proposals_to_adopt_or_abolish_daylight_saving_time">Proposals to adopt or abolish daylight saving time</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Daylight_saving_time_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Proposals to adopt or abolish daylight saving time">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>On 8 February 2018, the <a href="/wiki/European_Parliament" title="European Parliament">European Parliament</a> voted to ask the <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> to re-evaluate DST in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> After a web survey giving high support of not adjusting clocks twice annually<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> on 12 September 2018, the <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> decided to propose to put an end to seasonal clock changes (repealing Directive 2000/84/EC)<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> In order for this to be valid, the <a href="/wiki/European_Union_legislative_procedure" title="European Union legislative procedure">European Union legislative procedure</a> must be followed, mainly that the <a href="/wiki/Council_of_the_European_Union" title="Council of the European Union">Council of the European Union</a> and the European Parliament must both approve the proposal. </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Daylight_saving_time_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
